Sun Ke Issues Statement 125

A Managed Currency Standard is Difficult to Implement

The Situation in North China is Quite Worrying

Changing the Provincial System Will Have to Wait

According to the Central News Agency, Sun Ke, President of the Legislative Yuan, along with Navy Minister Chen Shaokuan, Vice Minister Liu Weichi, Vice Minister of Finance Zou Lin, and others, took the night train to Shanghai the night before last at 11 PM. They arrived at Zhenru at 7:20 AM yesterday morning and went straight to his private residence on Columbia Road to rest. A Central News Agency reporter visited Sun at his residence yesterday afternoon and recorded the following statement:

Situation in Eastern Chahar Has Now Eased 126

According to Sun, the situation in eastern Chahar was indeed very tense a few days ago, but it has gradually eased. As for our response measures, they will depend on the actions of the other side. The situation in North China is also quite worrying. Ambassador Yan has just arrived in Shanghai from North China, and you will have learned the details from Ambassador Yan himself.

A Managed Currency Standard is Difficult to Implement 127

The issue of our country adopting a managed currency standard has been decided by the National Economic Council and handed over to the Currency System Reform Committee of the Ministry of Finance for research. However, in my observation, it will be quite difficult for our country to adopt a managed currency standard. This is because whether the gold standard is applicable is still a question. If you look at various countries around the world, both the UK and the US have moved from the gold standard to a managed currency standard. Japan is also currently using a managed currency standard. Although France uses the gold standard, the currency circulating within the country is still paper money, and there is very little cash. Therefore, it is equivalent to a managed currency standard. From this, it can be seen that this is the trend of the world. If our country needs to adopt a managed currency standard, it must first have gold reserves and preparation. However, our country currently has no gold reserves or preparation at all. How can we implement a managed currency standard? If we want the Central Bank to issue banknotes to absorb cash, this will also be quite difficult. Therefore, in my observation, the issue of adopting a managed currency standard for our country is difficult to implement at present. But, as the trend of the world, the rise in silver prices will be difficult to avoid in the future. Our country urgently needs to plan for response measures to avoid economic panic in the future.

Discussions on Amending the Criminal Law in April 128

The Legislative Yuan is scheduled to begin discussing the draft amendment to the Criminal Law next month (April). As for the draft constitution, it has now been handed over to the review committee to solicit opinions from all parties and is scheduled to be submitted to the plenary session of the Legislative Yuan for discussion in mid-May. Legislative Committee member Wu Jingxiong, after being persuaded to stay, has now withdrawn his resignation. I have not heard of the rumors that Wu will take up an important position. It is likely not accurate. Minister Luo Wengan has been traveling south for a long time and should be able to return north soon.

The Issue of Abolishing Southwest Organs 129

Regarding the issue of changing the provincial system, it will have to wait until the provincial organization law is amended before it can be implemented. As for the issue of abolishing the Southwest Political Affairs Committee and the Southwest Executive Department, the central government has not formally discussed it. There may have been exchanges of opinions in private, but I am not aware of the details.

Yan Huiqing's Speech 130

Delivered at a Public Banquet Hosted by Three Organizations

Ambassador Yan Huiqing to Russia, is a senior figure in the diplomatic world. His arrival in Shanghai has been warmly welcomed by all sectors. Last night at 7:00 PM, the Shanghai YMCA, the International Problems Research Association, and the China Association for International Culture, jointly hosted a banquet on the ninth floor of the YMCA on Ba Xian Qiao Road. Over three hundred people attended, including Chinese and foreigners, such as Ying Zhongxi, Mu Ouchu, Tang Haian, Yan Deqing, Liu Dajun, Liu Hongsheng, Wang Jingqi, Li Zhaohuan, Lin Wojiang, Chen Liting, Cao Yunxiang, Li Zuchen, Yin Zhiling, Liu Yuwan, Lu Ganchen, Mr. and Mrs. Louis, Lai Huili, Bao Naide, and others. After the meal, Ambassador Yan delivered a speech, and the event concluded with a group photo at around 10:00 PM. Ambassador Yan's speech is as follows:

High Cost of Living in Europe and America 131

Two years ago, when I was ordered to serve as ambassador, after arriving in various countries in Europe and America, my first impression was the high cost of living there. For example, the luxurious, comfortable, all-steel passenger car I took from San Francisco to Washington was incredibly expensive, far beyond the dreams of the Chinese people. Not long after arriving in Washington, I received a telegram from the government urging me to attend a conference in Europe. The ocean liner from New York to France, with a displacement of 40,000 tons, took only four and a half days to travel that distance. I remember that thirty years ago, when I returned to China from America via Europe, the same distance took more than ten days. The speed of progress is unimaginable. The sophistication of the equipment and the high cost on the ship were also directly proportional. Later, in London, England, and Geneva, Switzerland, I felt the high cost of living everywhere. However, due to the global economic downturn, there were many unemployed people in various countries. It is estimated that there were over ten million in the United States and several million in the UK and Germany. Governments and people alike were feeling the pain and thought it unbearable. Looking back at our country, the number of unemployed people during normal times is probably no less than 50 million. In the past two years, it has probably reached 100 million. Yet, we seem to be indifferent. I have thought about the reason for this, and it is probably because our country's economic organization is far less sophisticated than that of Europe and America. Therefore, we have a sense of numbness. For example, a rickshaw that is not working well can be repaired simply and used勉强. But if a car engine is damaged, it must be carefully repaired in a factory.

Reasons for the Failure of International Conferences 132

The international conferences I attended, besides those concerning the Manchurian Incident, were the World Economic Conference and the Disarmament Conference. After returning to China this time, I often heard about the common problem of Chinese meetings, which is that they meet but don't discuss, discuss but don't decide, and decide but don't implement. European international conferences are slightly different. Every meeting discusses, and every decision is implemented. The difficulty lies in discussing but not deciding. The biggest reason for discussing but not deciding is that the participating countries inevitably have selfish intentions. They can't agree with each other and ultimately break down. For example, the World Economic Conference, at that time, people all over the world hoped for its success. On the opening day, the British King personally attended and delivered a speech, and the British Prime Minister served as the chairman. Representatives from various countries gathered together, and the atmosphere was lively and promising. However, everyone had their own agenda and was unwilling to sacrifice. In the end, a major conflict arose due to President Roosevelt's monetary policy, and it ended without much result. Its only achievement was the signing of the International Silver Agreement. After returning to China, I saw many articles about the silver agreement in newspapers and magazines. I am not an expert in finance or economics and dare not make any rash judgments. However, when I attended the Economic Conference with Minister Song at the time, I did give this matter some consideration. My only goal was to stabilize silver prices so that the ratio between gold and silver would not be too disparate. Speaking again of the Disarmament Conference, the reason why it has not been able to achieve results quickly is also because countries are unwilling to sacrifice. For example, naval powers hope to reduce land forces, and land powers hope to eliminate naval forces. Their opinions cannot be reconciled. The reason why they are still continuing to meet is that the people of all countries deeply hate war. If the government cannot敷衍 the public opinion advocating peace, it will be difficult to maintain its position.

The Soviet Union's National Austerity and Sacrifice 133

I was in the Soviet Union for only six months. With such a large country, after a superficial observation of six months, I would never dare say that I have any insights. However, we can have different views on the Soviet system, but we cannot deny the government's extraordinary efforts and the people's extraordinary sacrifices. During the outbreak of the European War, I was in Germany. The experiences and feelings I had at that time were almost the same as the experiences and feelings I had in the Soviet Union. In other words, the Soviet Union today is also in a national wartime mobilization era. Individuals cannot keep themselves warm or full, but their spirits are high and they are full of vitality. It is truly "臥薪嘗胆." Their aggressively managed new five-year plan, with the development of heavy industry as its first priority, employs thousands of foreign engineering experts to engage in guidance and design work, aiming to achieve success. This kind of hands-on, austere, and sacrificial spirit is worthy of the people of our country to imitate.

Efforts to Construct and Improve Material Well-being 134

On the way back to China, traveling east through the Suez Canal, I felt the backwardness of material construction in the East and the suffering of the people's livelihood. For example, our country is really too poor, and we should quickly think of ways to improve the material aspects. I often feel that apart from commercial hubs like Shanghai, material construction in our country is at least 150 years behind that of Europe and America. On the one hand, it is because the development of industries requires capital, and without sufficient capital, there is no way to start. On the other hand, it is also because the level of education among the people is too rudimentary. In the Soviet Union, every literate person is legally required to educate five or six other people. With the large number of illiterate people in our country, literate people should redouble their efforts to eliminate illiteracy. After being abroad for two years, I have many feelings about national affairs. The most optimistic thing is that the national government is working hard on construction. The National Economic Council's subsidies for various construction projects are indeed a matter of urgency and should be sincerely supported by the people of our country.

Still Optimistic About the League of Nations 135

Finally, I have one more thing I want to say to you. I am still optimistic about the future of the League of Nations. Many Chinese people have expressed their disappointment with the League of Nations because of the Manchurian Incident. However, as I have said before, the League of Nations is not a supreme government. As an organization with a national nature, with the absolute majority of its fifty member states speaking with one voice, advocating justice, saying: "Japan, you are wrong. China, you are right," it is truly an unprecedented event in history. Moreover, the scope of the League of Nations' activities is not limited to international political issues. Recently, it has paid considerable attention to cultural cooperation among countries. The reason why international disputes arise is that countries have not tried to understand each other, and 악감 feelings easily arise. If these feelings become too deep, war will inevitably break out. Therefore, a thorough solution lies in giving countries the opportunity for full cooperation. The importance of cultural cooperation lies here. Newspapers and books have a great influence in promoting this and the League of Nations pays great attention to them. I hope that those of you in the cultural field will promote them to contribute to world peace.

Four Organizations to Hold a Welcome Reception the Day After Tomorrow 136

The Association of Chinese Students in America, the Shanghai Universities Joint Association, the American Universities Association, and the Rotary Club of Shanghai, have decided to hold a welcome reception for Ambassador Yan Huiqing to Russia at the New Asia Hotel on North Sichuan Road at 7:30 PM on April 3rd and invite him to speak. Ambassador Yan has agreed. The welcome reception is being organized by four groups, and ladies are welcome to attend. The cost of the meal is two yuan. Please contact Mr. He Zhang or Mr. Li by phone at 81218 or 40040 before noon on Tuesday.

Wu Tiecheng, Li Shizeng, and Others Hosted a Public Farewell Dinner for Rajchman Yesterday 137

Dr. Rajchman, a technical liaison officer of the League of Nations, has made significant contributions since taking office in China. Because he urgently needs to go to Geneva to report to the League of Nations Administrative Council, he arrived in Shanghai from Nanjing the day before yesterday to prepare for his departure. Wu Tiecheng, the mayor of this city, Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, and the World Society and other groups, hosted a public farewell dinner for Rajchman at the World Society canteen on Ferguson Road last night at 7:00 PM. Song Ziwen, a member of the Standing Committee of the National Economic Council, and others were invited to accompany him. The dinner ended at around 9:00 PM.

City Federation of Trade Unions Hosted Morellet Yesterday 138

Morellet Hopes Chinese Workers Will Unite

Mr. Morellet, the Deputy Director of the International Labour Office, came to China to investigate cultural affairs and labour conditions. After arriving in Shanghai on the 16th of last month, he immediately went to Nanjing to exchange views with the Ministry of Education. After completing his business, he returned to Shanghai yesterday morning. The City Federation of Trade Unions hosted him at the YMCA on Ba Xian Qiao Road at 3:00 PM in the afternoon. Zhu Xuefan, Zhou Xuexiang, Long Peiyun from the City Federation of Trade Unions, Chen Zongcheng, the head of the Chinese branch of the International Labour Office, and representatives from various trade unions, totaling over sixty people, attended.

Chairman's Speech 139

First, the chairman, Zhu Xuefan, stood up to give a speech, stating that today, on behalf of the 400,000 organized workers in Shanghai, the federation is here to welcome Mr. Morellet, the Deputy Director of the International Labour Office, and requested Mr. Morellet to provide guidance on the Chinese workers' movement. He stated the main points of the welcome as follows: (1) The International Labour Organization has made many efforts to improve the lives of workers, which are worthy of our gratitude. (2) The world is facing an extreme economic crisis, and unemployment is serious. Various imperialist powers are also engaged in fierce arms races. Chinese workers are caught in this torrent and urgently need to save themselves. We hope that the International Labour Office will provide assistance. (3) Japan's constant aggression has caused China to suffer even more damage. Chinese workers must strive to make progress and join hands with workers around the world to overcome this difficulty and complete their historical mission to the country and the nation. (4) The urgent demands of Chinese workers today, such as foreign-owned factories in China complying with Chinese laws and Chinese workers residing abroad receiving the same treatment as workers in the host country, and the current implementation of factory inspection rights in Shanghai, are also hoped to be realized. We sincerely hope that Mr. Morellet can provide assistance on the above matters.

Mr. Morellet's Speech 140

Next, Mr. Morellet gave a speech. Here are some of the main points: (1) I am very pleased that the chairman said that 400,000 organized workers sympathize with the International Labour Organization. (2) Poverty makes society uneasy and the world chaotic. Therefore, in the future, we should strive to improve the lives of workers. Unemployment is severe today, indeed a famine. There are 300,000 statistically and about 10 million unstatistically. Including their families, there are tens of millions of people. Rescuing the suffering from unemployment is an urgent problem to be solved. The International Labour Office is working on it at all times. (3) Member states of the League of Nations are equal and cannot use imperialism to invade other countries. Although the International Labour Office is not a political organization, it is fundamentally opposed to imperialism. (4) Improving worker education and improving worker treatment are essential. I hope that the workers of your country can unite to help the International Labour Office overcome difficulties. Finally, he expressed his deep gratitude for today's welcome.

Post Office Welcomes 141

A letter from the National Postal Workers' General Union to Mr. Morel reads: Respected Sir, the International Labour Office has been working for the liberation of workers worldwide for more than a decade, with remarkable achievements. All workers deeply admire it. Now, your esteemed Deputy Director has travelled a long distance to our country to inspect the situation of workers, intending to contribute his sincere advice and grand plans to improve the status of Chinese workers. We are deeply grateful. Our union is the general organization of 30,000 postal workers nationwide. In recent years, we have worked tirelessly to protect the treatment of workers, develop postal services, and contribute to the country and society. We have achieved considerable records in the history of the workers' movement. However, the promotion of world peace depends heavily on the unity of international workers. Therefore, in addition to our warm welcome and sincere gratitude, we deeply hope that your esteemed Deputy Director will uphold the spirit of promoting the international workers' movement, not forsake the distance, and provide guidance, so that the happiness of our union members, the unity of international workers, and world peace can be improved day by day, and the welfare of workers will be truly relied upon. Enclosed are several publications of our union for your kind reference. We are deeply grateful. Sincerely, The National Postal Workers' General Union of China, together with Lu Jingshi, Zhu Xuefan, Zhao Shusheng, Zhang Kechang, Wang Xuansheng, Fan Caicong, Shui Xiangyun, and Xu Ziqin, representatives of the Shanghai Postal Workers' Union, respectfully submit this on March 31st.

US President's Fondness for Chinese Tea 142

Envoy Tuo Shih requested to purchase fine products

The Central News Agency reports: There is a very interesting piece of news here, stating that US President Roosevelt is particularly fond of Qimen tribute black tea from China. He serves Qimen tea to guests at home as the finest product. The reason is that Mrs. Roosevelt's grandfather used to work for the American company Lao Qichang in Shanghai. The company dealt with the export of Chinese tea. Therefore, he would send the highest quality black tea home during festivals. President Roosevelt became addicted to it. Before becoming president, he would send people to China to purchase fine products. After becoming president, due to busy schedules, the needs increased. He then personally requested our envoy to the United States, Shih Zhaoji, to purchase fine products on his behalf. Now, Envoy Shih has entrusted the Qimen tribute product, which participated in the Chicago Centennial Exposition, and still requested Envoy Shih to forward it for trial drinking.

Three Propaganda Vehicles Specially Arranged

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration has scheduled today (April 1st) to hold a system-wide hygiene campaign. The bureau has specially prepared three propaganda vehicles, attached to the rear of passenger trains, to depart and promote the campaign at various stations: (1) Attached to train No. 12 from Shanghai North to Changzhou; (2) Attached to train No. 11 from Nanjing to Changzhou; (3) Attached to train No. 37 from Shanghai North to Zha Kou. The implementation details are as follows: (A) Station Arrangements: 1. Raising flags; 2. Hanging banners and illustrated slogans. (B) Cleaning: 1. General cleaning: All stations, factories, train yards, offices and dormitories, Rotary schools, and trains of the two railways will hold general cleaning. 2. Rectifying tea houses and vendors: The tea houses and vendors at the stations of the two railways, although usually attentive, can further rectify at this time, so that the products, utensils, clothing, and the service providers themselves can be improved, and the concepts and interests of hygiene can be increased significantly. This may yield excellent results in the future. 3. Rectifying dining cars and tea servers: Most of the waiters and tea servers in the dining cars maintain the status quo and lack initiative in hygiene habits. If they are fully rectified at this opportunity, they can be completely reformed. (C) Promotion: 1. Text: Compile and print special issues on hygiene campaigns, as well as illustrations, brochures, leaflets, and slogans on hygiene and prevention of seasonal epidemics, and distribute them to various departments, stations, machine shops, trains, and passengers. 2. Lectures: Give popular lectures to passengers and railway employees. (D) Inspection: The section chiefs of the police sections of the two railways, together with the station masters of each station, will organize inspection teams to go to various stations, vehicles, machine shops, factories, offices, dormitories, and Rotary schools to conduct cleaning inspections and be responsible for maintaining order at the event. (E) Healthcare: 1. Vaccination: The health department will issue a notice to the hospitals and clinics of the two railways to provide vaccination to employees and their families, station passengers, and residents along the railway line. 2. Typhoid vaccination: The health department will issue a notice to the hospitals and clinics of the two railways to provide typhoid vaccination to employees and their families, station passengers, and residents along the railway line.

Rent Reduction Association Representatives Petitioned the Municipal Government Yesterday 147

Yu Hongjun Received Them and Expressed Rent Reduction Measures

Should be Discussed by a Joint Meeting of Party and Government Agencies, the Municipal Council, and Mass Organizations

Petition Representatives 148

Each car was inserted with a white cloth flag with the words "Rent Reduction Association Petition Group", which was quite noticeable.

Satisfactory Result 149

After the petition group arrived at the municipal government, Mayor Wu happened to have important official business and sent Secretary-General Yu Hongjun to meet them. Chen Jiufeng, the representative of the group, explained the purpose of the petition to Yu. Yu immediately stated that at this time of market depression and business decline, rent reduction seemed necessary, but this matter was of great importance and should be discussed and resolved by a joint meeting of party and government agencies, the municipal council, and mass organizations. He hoped that the representatives would convey this message and encourage the citizens to wait patiently for a solution. The representatives were satisfied and returned to the association by car and dispersed. It is reported that the Rent Reduction Association has scheduled a meeting of representatives of various organizations at 2:00 PM on Tuesday, April 3, to report on the petition.

Jiang Feng Machine Did Not Depart Yesterday Due to Fog 150

Postponed Flight to Fujian This Morning

The Jiang Feng seaplane manufactured by the Naval Aircraft Manufacturing Office was originally scheduled to be flown by instructor Xu Chengqi along the coast to Fuzhou from the water airport on the Longhua River at 8:00 AM yesterday to test the long-distance flight capability of the aircraft. The fog completely cleared at 11:00 AM, but it was too late to reach the destination on the same day. Therefore, it was decided to postpone the departure to 7:00 AM this morning.

Wireless Radio Combination Starts Today 151

Colleagues from the Wireless Radio Main Station

Petition to Abolish the Director System

The news of the joint operation of wired and wireless radio has been widely publicized for a long time. The telegram bureau and the wireless radio main station in this city have received an order from the Ministry of Communications to mutually receive and send reports from the receiving and sending offices of both sides from April 1st. In addition, wireless radio stations in various places, except for the economy, are still allowed to be independent, and must be subject to the command and supervision of the local telegraph bureau director. It is heard that all the staff of the wireless radio main station in this city believe that the director system of the telegraph bureau has long been criticized by the world. Now, regardless of qualifications and achievements, making all radio stations in the country subject to the command of the director not only easily leads to disputes, but also enough to make the business worse. A telegram was sent to the Ministry of Communications yesterday, requesting the abolition of the director system, and at the time of the joint operation, strict methods should be established and strictly restricted to prevent problems before they occur. The original telegram is recorded below: Minister and Deputy Minister of the Ministry of Communications of Nanjing, Director of the Directorate General of Telecommunications, Your Excellencies, we believe that the joint operation of wired and wireless radio is indeed an important plan to improve telecommunications administration. Now, Your Excellency's telegram orders that from April 1st, wireless radio stations, except for the economy, are still allowed to be independent, and all are under the command and supervision of the wired radio bureau director. We have something to say that we cannot help but say. I would like to elaborate on this to you. The director system of the telegraph bureau has long been criticized by the world. It should be among Your Excellency's insights. Telecommunications is a business nature, and the director is a government official system, which was originally incompatible. In the past, during the warlord era, these directors were mostly appointed by the warlords first, and then the old Ministry of Communications would appoint them again. Under this kind of compromising situation, a situation of separatism was formed, so that the old Ministry of Communications could not intervene in the bureau's affairs and finances. As a result, arbitrary actions were taken, private individuals were employed, and things like cronyism were endless. Even embezzling public funds and absconding were all possible. Today, there are not a few directors who are wanted and at large. The influence of the old telegraph bureau on the world (omitted) is undeniable. Moreover, from the perspective of telecommunications itself, it was originally a group of various technical personnel, and specialized talents should be selected and managed scientifically. Therefore, we changed to the engineer system at the beginning of the establishment of the wireless radio station, so that ambitious warlords could not hijack it, and the uneducated and ignorant could not covet it. The reason why the national radio stations are still energetic and disciplined is by no means accidental. Now, at the beginning of the joint operation, the system is not determined, the organization is not prepared, and a piece of telegram orders all radio stations in the country to be subject to the command and supervision of the directors of various bureaus. Regardless of whether the qualifications and experience of the directors of various places are above the engineers of each station, it is still questionable. Moreover, there have been many disputes between bureaus and stations due to business relations in the past, and it is not difficult to review them. Now, regardless of qualifications and achievements, forcibly ordering them to be subject to their command, then on the one hand, in addition to being complacent and arrogant, arbitrarily arranging things is in their mind. It is inevitable that conflicts will occur and business will be ruined. Why should you say it again? Is this not the original intention of Your Excellency's joint operation? Therefore, the director system must be abolished in the future. For the current transition, it is especially necessary to establish strict methods and strictly restrict them, so that the power of command is still unified in the department and division, so as to prevent problems before they occur. Moreover, the directors currently appointed by Your Excellency are honest, self-loving, and specialized talents, then at the time of the joint operation, they can be separately changed and checked into technical reporting personnel. In the future, select the best to be appointed to the position of主管电信机关, and for the sake of thoroughly reforming telecommunications administration, it seems appropriate to stipulate that special-grade and first-grade agencies should set up chief engineers as the统辖 personnel, and those of the second and third grades and below should set up directors, who should be selected and promoted from technical reporting personnel or business personnel with matching qualifications. If so, the telecommunications agency will be entirely governed by specialized talents, and the business prospects will be promising. The views of our 等 are humble and there are many errors, but out of the enthusiasm for protecting telecommunications administration, we venture to state them. We respectfully ask you to review, decide, and implement them. Telecommunications is fortunate, and we 等 are fortunate. Staff of the Shanghai Wireless Radio Main Station respectfully bow,世,

Railway Bureau Ordered to Deal with Wusong Factory Strike Case 152

Ten Directors Arrested

Factory Director of the Machine Factory Changed

The Central News Agency reports that the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration issued a message saying that in December of last year, when the central government was suppressing the Fujian rebellion and martial law was in effect in Shanghai, the Wusong Machine Factory branch of the railway trade union accused Mo Heng, director of the General Affairs Department and the Materials Department. At the same time, the workers of the machine factory and the Wusong Materials Factory suddenly went on strike. The Ministry of Railways has instructed to handle it according to law. The bureau has separately notified the special party department and the trade union of the railway, and at the same time announced it to the public. The details are as follows:

Cause of the Case 153

In December of last year, Mo Heng, director of the General Affairs Department and the Materials Department of the Railway Bureau, transferred Cao Wenkui, an employee of the Wusong Materials Department, to Ningbo to serve. Cao also served as the director of the branch office of the two railway trade unions. The trade union members believed that Director Mo's move was to divide the power of the trade union and intentionally undermine the workers' movement. They accused Director Mo of undermining the workers' movement, slandering the party department for engaging in private corruption, and other charges to the railway bureau and the Ministry of Railways, and went on strike to force Director Mo to be expelled. The Railway Bureau consulted with the two railway party departments to give good guidance, and submitted a request to the ministry for instructions on how to handle it. The ministry sent personnel to the railway to thoroughly investigate and advised them to resume work. Soon, the workers also followed the advice and resumed work first, waiting for the ministry to deal with it.

Ministry Ordered to Handle 154

After thoroughly investigating the truth and studying it in detail, the Ministry of Railways instructed the Railway Bureau to handle it in three points: (1) There is no evidence to support the original accusations, and they should be dismissed without discussion. (2) Director Mo's imprudent remarks caused misunderstandings and should be reprimanded. (3) The workers of the department did not wait for a legal resolution and went on strike to force them to comply. Cao Wenkui has not yet complied with the transfer to Ningbo, which is inappropriate and should be dealt with according to law. The bureau should follow Article 30 of the Railway Employee Service Regulations, which states, "Employees who take the opportunity to gather crowds for strikes or delays, or gather crowds to force compliance and disrupt order, shall be dismissed and prosecuted by the court according to their leaders and followers. During military martial law, they may also be punished according to military law." After reporting to the Ministry of Railways, they were ordered by the Ministry of Railways to inform them by telegram on a specific date. It has been forwarded to the Military Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, who replied with two points: (1) Cao Wenkui should be punished by the Shanghai Garrison Command to the fullest extent of the law. (2) If the Wusong Machine Factory attempts to strike again, the Shanghai Security Team will be dispatched by the Shanghai Garrison Command to strictly suppress it. The bureau has followed the order on March 30 and separately notified the special party department and the trade union of the railway. The Shanghai Garrison Command has also dispatched the Shanghai Security Team to be stationed in Wusong to protect the machine factory and its employees. Although the workers of the machine factory and the Wusong Materials Factory who echoed the strike should be dismissed according to law, they are treated leniently.

Railway Bureau Announcement 155

The Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration announced that in December of last year, the workers of the Wusong Machine Factory and the Wusong Materials Factory went on strike for as long as a week, causing huge losses to the railway, and also incited other workers to respond. At that time, the central government was suppressing the Fujian rebellion and martial law was in effect in Shanghai. The military transportation of the two railways was very important. It was reported that there were reactionary elements manipulating them, trying to undermine the overall situation. The Ministry of Railways has instructed that this strike should be handled according to law. In addition to transferring the employees who instigated the strike on that day to the Shanghai Garrison Command for investigation and punishment according to the order of the Military Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in accordance with Article 30 of the Railway Employee Service Regulations, all workers of the two railways who participated in the strike should also be dismissed and prosecuted in accordance with Article 30 of the Railway Employee Service Regulations. They are treated leniently because of their ignorance and being deceived. The Machine Department and the Materials Department have been ordered to admonish them earnestly. They should continue to work normally with peace of mind and sincerity, and do not need to be suspicious and afraid. But if they do not cherish themselves and are incited by others, and have excessive actions, they will only be reported to the Shanghai Garrison Command and severely suppressed in accordance with the order of the Military Commission Chairman Chiang Kai-shek. Other workers who were not incited and did not participate in the strike at that time are not related to this case. They should uphold the original intention of loving the railway and the country, abide by discipline, and work seriously. This is very important. This announcement.

Trade Union Urgent Telegram 156

The New Sound News Agency reported that the two railway trade unions telegraphed the two railway special party departments, stating that according to reports, at about 10:00 AM today, Wang, the director of the Machine Department of the Two Railway Administration, notified all directors of the Wusong Machine Factory branch of the trade union to go to the meeting room in the North Station for talks. However, when the directors arrived at the North Station, they were taken to the Shanghai Garrison Command by armed railway police. Except for directors Zhu Derong and Tang Dafa, who were sick and did not arrive, the other directors, Cao Wenkui, Han Weiyu, Li Kuiyuan, Chen Shusheng, Shi Zhenyuan, Tang Genfa, He Laixing, Lin Jinlin, Xu Shanqing, and Zhou Weixian, ten people in total, were all arrested and have not been released yet, and the facts are unclear and the reasons are unknown. In order to telegraph and ask your association to quickly find a way to bail them out and avoid harming the innocent, the Railway Union directly under the Ministry of Railways in Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou and Ningbo bowed, printed.

Change of Factory Director 157

The New New News Agency reported that Mao Erwei, the director of the Wusong Machine Factory, was suspended from his post by the Bureau on the morning of the 31st, and Chen Fuhai, the chief engineer of the Shanghai-Hangzhou Longtoufang of the Two Railway Machine Departments, was appointed to replace him.

Lawyer Yan Luqing Accused of Insulting the Court 167

Many Disputes in the Huang Chujiu Estate Case

Lawyer Yan Loudly Reads the Judge is a Living Buddha

The Jiangsu Shanghai Second Special District Court, due to the issue of auctioning off real estate mortgaged to the Wanchun Silver Group and the China Industrial Bank in the Huang Chujiu estate debt case, summoned lawyers representing various creditors and debtors to court on February 23rd, presided over by Judge Cao Jun of the Enforcement Chamber, for a hearing. The court intended to have a portion of Huang's mortgaged property valued and handed over to the mortgagees. Consequently, a portion of ordinary creditors...

...the draft report submitted by his client contained a passage saying, "The judge is like a living Buddha, and the mortgage creditors have reached a settlement with the president of the court to receive the proceeds from the auction," etc. The court, considering Lawyer Yan Luqing's actions to be obstructing official duties and intentionally insulting the court, transferred the case to the Prosecutor's Office. Prosecutor Wang Ren summoned Lawyer Yan Luqing to court for investigation. As a result, he believed that Yan was indeed suspected of insult and filed a public prosecution with the same-level court in accordance with Article 146 of the Criminal Law. The court issued a summons, and Yan appeared in court yesterday. At 10:00 AM, Judge Sun Pengxian, together with Prosecutor Wang Ren and Clerk Chen Boyan, specially opened the Sixth Court for trial. In court, the judge first inquired about the defendant's age and origin. Then, the prosecutor stood up and stated the intention of the prosecution. The judge asked Yan Luqing, "On February 23rd, during the court session for the late Huang Chujiu's estate debt case, did you loudly read the draft report when the enforcement judge was presiding over the hearing? When the enforcement judge told you not to read it, did you ignore him and continue reading?" Yan replied, "That's not right. There were special circumstances. Firstly, this request in the report was urgently related to the case. Secondly, the court had not yet received this report. Thirdly, the original handwriting of the draft was unclear, so I was afraid the judge couldn't see it clearly. Therefore, I asked the judge to issue the draft for me to read." The judge asked, "Does the report contain a passage saying, 'The judge is a living Buddha, no different from a puppet,' and 'The Wanchun Silver Group and the China Industrial Bank have reached a settlement with the president of the court,' etc.? Was it intentional insult?" Yan replied, "The client sent this draft to my office a few days ago. However, my request was entirely for the purpose of not issuing funds to the Wanchun Silver Group. When reading the draft, I inadvertently read this passage. It was due to the circumstances and not intentional insult." The judge asked, "Did Judge Cao prohibit you from reading the draft when you were reading it?" Yan replied, "No." The judge said that there was a clerk's record as evidence today. Yan replied, "Although there is this statement, I did not read this record at the time and did not sign it." The judge asked, "When you were reading the draft, did you feel that you were insulting the court?" Yan replied, "I didn't think of it at the time. Only now do I realize that it was slightly inappropriate." However, the defendant has always respected the court, has no personal or public animosity, and has no conflict of interest. How could I have the intention to insult? After questioning, the judge ordered the debate to begin. Prosecutor Wang stood up to argue, stating that the defendant in this case, in court, loudly read that Judge Cao was a living Buddha, no different from a puppet, and that the Wanchun Silver Group and the China Industrial Bank had reached a settlement with the president of the court, etc., which was indeed an insult and should be judged in accordance with Article 146 of the Criminal Law. The defendant, Yan Luqing, did not retain a lawyer and defended himself, stating that he read it because the handwriting of the draft report was not clear when the enforcement chamber was in session. The clerk's record of Judge Cao saying that I read it loudly is not accurate. Please note that the defendant usually detests rumors. This time, the client came to me and mentioned this rumor. I immediately tried to refute its absurdity. As for reading the entire report in court, it cannot be discussed as a rumor. Moreover, reading the report is a legitimate act. If the court cannot read the statement of claim, then where can it be read? To be prosecuted and deemed a criminal for a lawyer reading a statement of claim is unexpected. If the judge believed that there was something illegal in reading the statement of claim at the time, he could have prohibited it. However, the defendant started handling this case with great enthusiasm, solely and wholeheartedly to safeguard the rights and property of the client from danger. Therefore, I requested that this statement be issued for me to read, and I inadvertently read the passage about the judge and the president. I never expected to be a defendant today. Moreover, Article 1 of the Criminal Law states that an act is not a crime if there is no explicit penalty in the law at the time of the act. Article 24 states that non-intentional acts are not punishable. Article 34 states that acts performed in accordance with the law or legitimate acts in the course of legitimate business are not punishable. Article 36 states that acts of defense against present unlawful infringement of one's own or another's rights are not punishable. Article 37 states that acts of necessity in order to rescue oneself or another from imminent danger to life, body, freedom, or property are not punishable. I request that the court reject the public prosecution and declare the defendant not guilty, etc. After the debate, the court announced the end of the debate and adjourned the hearing to a scheduled sentencing.

Landlord Fails in Attempt to Increase Rent at Shoupin Lane 169

No Reason for Rent Increase

Plaintiff Loses Lawsuit Yesterday

The houses in Shoupin Lane on Huade Road in Yangshupu originally belonged to the Yipin Bank. The rent was increased once in March of the 19th year of the Republic of China (1930). At that time, the tenants and the owner signed a contract stating that the rent could only be increased or decreased after the end of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), and only with the consent of both parties. Later, Yipin sold the property to others. The new owner commissioned the Gao Yi Real Estate Agency to manage the property. In November of last year, the agency notified all tenants of a rent increase. The rent for each market house, originally 22 yuan, would be increased by 29 yuan, requiring a monthly payment of 51 yuan. The rent for each lane house, originally 18 yuan, would be increased by 13 yuan, requiring a monthly payment of 31 yuan. The rent for double houses, originally 40 yuan, would be increased by 33 yuan, requiring a monthly payment of 73 yuan. The tenants, citing the previous contract, stated that the period for increasing or decreasing the rent had not yet arrived. Moreover, with the economic downturn in recent years, citizens were requesting rent reductions to ease their burden. The owner, on the contrary, wanted to violate the contract and increase the rent at this time, which was purely self-serving. After a meeting of all the tenants, they specially hired lawyer Yuan Yang'an to negotiate with the Gao Yi Real Estate Agency, demanding that they respect the previous agreement, consider the people's livelihood, and cancel the rent increase proposal. Negotiations broke down last month. Gao Yi Real Estate Agency then filed a lawsuit against all the tenants in the First Special District Court, requesting that the court order the tenants to move out and return the houses. During the court hearing, lawyer Yuan, representing the tenants, argued based on the contract, rental customs, and the fact that the landlord could not force the tenants to move out if they did not owe more than three months' rent. He debated with the plaintiff's lawyer, Lu Xingyuan, requesting that the plaintiff's lawsuit be rejected. The presiding judge, Qiao Wanxuan, has now announced the judgment, stating that the plaintiff's claims are groundless and should be dismissed, and the plaintiff should bear the litigation costs.

Zhou E'xuan Sued for Confirmation of Biological Son 170

Jurisdiction Error, Transferred to Local Court for Trial

Zhou E'xuan, the eldest son of Zhou Weishi, owner of the Zhou Gengji Yarn Store, a wealthy merchant from Suzhou living in Shanghai, was sued by Zhang Zhuying, the mother of his biological son, Dayuan, in the name of the child's legal guardian, for abandoning Dayuan and failing to provide support. She hired a lawyer to file a criminal self-accusation against Zhou E'xuan, requesting that the defendant be punished in accordance with Article 309 of the Criminal Law. After repeated summons by the First Special District Court, the defendant flatly denied it. The court then sent the plaintiff, defendant, and the boy Dayuan to the Zhenru Forensic Research Institute for identification. The results confirmed that Dayuan was indeed the biological son of Zhou E'xuan and Zhang Zhuying, as reported in this newspaper. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Wu Xiangzu held a continued hearing. The defendant's lawyer first stated the reason for requesting a stay of proceedings, saying in brief that if the defendant and the child did have a filial relationship, then a self-accusation would not be legally possible. However, the defendant has always denied that the child was born to him, so the point of contention in this case is actually the question of recognition or denial. This question should be resolved by the civil court. The defendant has now submitted a petition for mediation, requesting mediation. It is expected that the mediation will not be successful and a lawsuit to deny the relationship will have to be filed. In order to comply with the procedure, the personal lawsuit should be resolved first, and then the criminal case. Therefore, he requested that the case be stayed. The plaintiff's lawyer stood up to object, saying that the defendant's request was too late, as the case had now entered the trial phase. The request made by the defendant should have been made during the investigation. Judge Wu then questioned Zhou E'xuan, who stated that the mediation petition was sent to the court on the 26th. The judge then declared that according to the law, a personal lawsuit that has not been formally filed cannot be used to request a stay of proceedings in another case. However, if the defendant in this case constitutes a crime, then the crime committed should be a violation of Article 310, which should be handled by the local court. He immediately wrote the judgment: "This case is a jurisdiction error and should be transferred to the local court for handling." Defendant Zhou E'xuan paid 20,000 yuan in cash as bail.

Customs Controls Foreign Towing Barges 175

Effective Today

The Inspector General of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, Mr. Mayers, previously submitted a request to the Ministry of Finance for interpretation regarding whether the towing barge regulations apply to foreign towing barges and whether a reasonable period should be granted for implementation. The Ministry of Finance forwarded the request to the Ministry of Communications. It is now learned that the Ministry of Communications, after considering the situation, has explained that the Ministry of Foreign Affairs was consulted on the issue of whether or not to issue licenses to foreign towing barges. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs stated that issuing licenses does not conflict with current treaties. Contact was also made with the Ministry of Finance, which stated that the Customs had stopped issuing towing barge licenses since the implementation of the Towing Barge Management Regulations on November 1st of the 22nd year of the Republic of China (1933), with the approval of the Ministry of Finance. Since issuing licenses to foreign towing barges does not conflict with treaties and the Customs has stopped issuing licenses, all the regulations stipulated in the Towing Barge Management Regulations issued by the Ministry of Communications should apply to foreign towing barges. All instructions in the Ministry's No. 6407 order last year, "However, foreign vessels do not need to apply for towing barge licenses," should be canceled. The period for the Customs to implement control over foreign towing barges should be extended to April 1st of this year.

The Business Offices of Both Railways Reduce Luggage Handling Fees 180

A Flat Rate of Twenty-Five Cents Per Piece

The business offices of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have been operating very successfully. In particular, the freight business has been most developed, which is convenient to the society and leads to sharp increases in business income. Recently, luggage handling fees have been reduced, and direct issuance of parcel receipts has been implemented, which is very optimistic for the business development. The details are as follows:

Monthly Operating Revenue Exceeds 40,000 Yuan. Since its opening, the operating revenue of the office has been increasing monthly. The monthly income for January and February of this year both exceeded 40,000 yuan. The income for this month is expected to be even more considerable, with an average daily business of about 1,400 yuan. Both the Beijing office and the Nanshi branch office have also made progress.

Significant Reduction in Luggage Handling Fees. The original rate for the office to pick up and deliver luggage for customers was 40 cents per piece, 35 cents per piece for 10 to 19 pieces, 30 cents per piece for 20 to 29 pieces, and 25 cents per piece for 30 pieces or more. Now, the office considers that most ordinary passengers have fewer than 10 pieces of luggage, and charging 40 cents per piece may be slightly high. Therefore, it has been approved that the rate will be reduced to 25 cents per piece starting from April 1st. There is no separate loading and unloading fee at the North Station.

Parcel Receipts Can Be Obtained Immediately. The parcel business of the office is growing daily. In the past, customers had to send parcels to the office, which then had to be transferred to the North Station to issue official receipts and send them to customers. The procedures were complicated and prone to delays. It has now been decided to install scales in the office, so that customers can obtain receipts immediately after sending parcels to the office, which is very convenient. This new plan is currently being prepared and will be implemented soon.

Since the January 28th Incident, the original rent has been calculated at 83%. Recently, due to the sluggish market and difficult livelihoods, the tenants in this lane have requested rent reductions from the landlord, but without results. The landlord has understood and appointed representative Fan Hengde to negotiate peaceful solutions with the lane representatives. Finally, it was decided that starting from February of this year, the current rent will be calculated at 90%. Both parties have reached a compromise. The original rent for the houses in this lane was 83% after the war, and now it is 90%, which is not much different from the rent reduction methods decided by the city-wide rent reduction meeting. Ministry of Finance Orders Import Tax on Coal Oil and Gasoline to be Increased Starting Today 191

Customs Announces Tax Rate Notice to Begin Collection

Annual Increase of 10 Million Possible After Tax Increase

Coal oil and gasoline are not produced in our country, but they are necessary for the people of a boat and for industrial use. Japan and our country are in a similar situation, and the government taxes are particularly light to reduce the burden on the people. Because our country's finances are not on track and expenditures are in short supply, there is no other way but to increase taxes to make up for the shortfall. After a long period of careful consideration, the government has determined a new tax rate and will first try it out. The reporter of Shenshi News Agency specially investigated and recorded the various situations as follows:

Ministry of Finance Orders Commencement 192

Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi has always adhered to the policy of increasing revenue and reducing expenditure, and rectifying national tax revenue in order to stabilize finances and put them on track. The annual import volume of coal oil and gasoline is very large, and a slight increase in the tax rate can increase the annual revenue by 10 million yuan, which is indeed a shortcut to increasing revenue. The tax increase has been under consideration for a long time in order to increase revenue, but it was slightly frustrated by opposition from the Legislative Yuan and other parties. It has now been realized. It is learned that the Ministry of Finance secretly ordered the Jianghai Customs Superintendent and the Chief Tax Officer five days ago to issue a notice that, starting from April 1, the amended coal oil, gasoline, and type B diesel tax rates determined by the Ministry of Finance will be temporarily implemented according to the new rules. Jianghai Customs Superintendent Tang Haian and Customs Tax Officer Bolede issued notices in Chinese and foreign newspapers today to implement the order.

Customs Issues Notice to Commence Collection 193

The Jianghai Customs has issued a notice to temporarily implement the amended coal oil, gasoline, and type B diesel tax rates, and today issued Notice No. 1351, which was sent to Chinese and foreign newspapers for publication. The reporter of Shenshi News Agency has found and recorded the notice as follows: Jianghai Customs issues Notice No. 1351 to temporarily implement the amended coal oil, gasoline, and type B diesel tax rates. Now, in accordance with the order of the Ministry of Finance, starting from April 1 of this year, the amended import tariff rates for coal oil and diesel will be temporarily implemented as follows: No. 520 Mineral, gasoline, naphthenic gasoline, and aromatic gasoline (including various unspecified engine fuels) (A) Boxed, two cans per box, each can 18.93 liters, or 5 US gallons, 2.10 gold units, (B) Bulk, 10 liters, 0.53 gold units, No. 532 Kerosene, (including other mineral oils for ignition with a specific gravity of 0.78 to 0.90) (A) Boxed, two cans per box, each can 18.93 kilograms, or 5 US gallons, 1.80 gold units, (B) Bulk, 10 liters 0.45 gold units, No. 529 Diesel, (B) Other (including crude oil for refining) 33.60 gold units per tonne, (Note) For diesel imports with a kerosene content of more than 60%, the principle of proportionate taxation applies. The customs will verify the actual kerosene content and levy diesel tax at a rate of 33.60 gold units per tonne for 60% kerosene content, but limited to 80% kerosene content. Also, for kerosene refined in Guangdong and Guangxi and transported to other provinces, in addition to the transit tax and surtax, the import tax should also be supplemented. The tax rates are as follows: No. 532 Kerosene, (A) Boxed, two cans per box, each can 18.93 liters, or 5 US gallons, 1.55 gold units (B) Bulk, 10 liters, 0.41 gold units. All merchants should be aware of this and are hereby notified. March 31, 23rd year of the Republic of China, Superintendent Tang Haian, Tax Officer Bolede.

Import Oil Volume Statistics 194

Li Chunsheng was also involved in the shooting death of Xie Abao, the head of the Nei Wai Cotton Mill in Putuo Road on December 12 of the 18th year of the Republic of China, and in the armed attack on Wu Wanzhang, the factory inspector from Hubei, near Youdeli on Putuo Road on December 25 of the 15th year of the Republic of China, with the intent to harm his life. They were sent to the First Special District Court. Li Chunsheng hired lawyer Fan Gang to defend him. They were ordered to await sentencing. Judge Bei Xiecai presided over the Second Criminal Division and sentenced Cao Zhenxi to one year and two months of imprisonment, and Xu Debiao and Du Baoliang to three years and six months each. The number of days of detention before the final judgment were deducted from the term of imprisonment at a rate of two days for each day of imprisonment. The firearms and ammunition were confiscated. Li Chunsheng Tang Xuyou and Yuan Xingfu were found not guilty. Li Chunsheng's murder charges were postponed for a joint hearing with the arrested offender Xia Shaoqiu and others.
