Reading Q&A

How to Study the Constitution 208

The following discusses several main issues in our Constitution:

(1) Land Issue: Even scholars of the scholar-official class acknowledge that land rent is an unearned income, the increase in land value is a result of social development, and land harvest is the product of tenant farmers' hard work. Landowners' compensation for land can be said to be entirely due to the social system rather than any contribution or sacrifice made by the individual to the land. In advanced industrial countries, because industrial forces dominate, this issue does not seem serious, but it cannot be said to be completely resolved. In backward countries like ours, the land issue is an urgent problem facing us, especially because of the rural economic bankruptcy in recent years, which has further exposed the suffering of tenant farmers. Their land harvests cannot be sold at a good price, yet they still have to pay rent. Therefore, even though many people are thinking of superficial remedies, they are still moving towards decline day by day. Most people do not realize that the core of this problem is production, and politically, it is the vast number of farmers demanding land and improving production methods to develop agricultural productivity. Therefore, if we consider the development of the entire society, this problem cannot be ignored.

According to the current solution, in principle, land is jointly owned by the public. However, on the other hand, it also stipulates that those who have legally acquired ownership still have ownership. Therefore, this principle of "joint ownership by the public" is even more empty than "sovereignty belongs to the entire people." If the land is privately owned, then why is it also jointly owned? Even if it is said that the increase in land value can be heavily taxed by the state, and its benefits can be shared by all the people rather than enjoyed exclusively by the owners? However, whether the state's interests can be equally enjoyed by all the people is still a question. Moreover, the increase in land price is a secondary issue. The focus is whether the general farmers can fully enjoy the harvest of their labor in using the land. Therefore, legislators should seriously consider this issue and stipulate appropriate principles in the Constitution.

(2) Nationalities Issue: With the unbalanced development of industry across regions, there is a distinction between advanced and backward nationalities. As a result of mass production, there has been the fact of national oppression. Moreover, due to the crisis of capitalism itself, advanced countries are increasingly fierce in their oppression and exploitation of minority nationalities or backward nationalities within their own countries. Therefore, the issue of minority nationalities should have detailed provisions in the Constitution to safeguard the spirit of national self-determination and reduce the generation of national conflicts. There are two such safeguards: (1) Strictly guarantee the equal political participation rights of minority nationalities. The number of representatives to the National Assembly from each nationality should be equal, and each nationality should have the right to handle its own political affairs. (2) The principle of national equality alone is not enough, and the phenomenon of national discrimination is still unavoidable. Therefore, it should be stipulated that each nationality has the right to independence. This is a prerequisite for implementing the spirit of national self-determination and should not be ignored. Some argue that if the right to independence is clearly defined, minority nationalities will be incited by imperialism to split, and after the split, the minority nationalities will inevitably become colonies of imperialism. In fact, this is unfounded worry, and this will never happen in reality. If all nationalities within the country can be truly equal, there will never be a split. Imperialism will not only fail to incite the separation of minority nationalities but will also strengthen their determination to unite and jointly form a solid anti-imperialist alliance. Conversely, if close ties cannot be established and a few nobles among the minority nationalities are used, separation will still be unavoidable even without this provision. When the Soviet Union recognized the right to independence of all minority nationalities in the Declaration of Laborers, each minority nationality felt oppressed by the past Tsarist government and declared independence one after another. However, after independence, due to the threat of imperialism, they still united into a large federation. Our country does not recognize the right of national separation, but there have been serious national conflicts such as the independence of Xinjiang and the demand for autonomy in Inner Mongolia. In short, mutual trust and cooperation between nationalities depend on whether there are objective conditions for trust and cooperation. To guarantee the spirit of national equality, the right to independence must be stipulated.

(3) Livelihood Issue: Labor-capital disputes and tens of millions of unemployed people are the main symptoms of today's society. The key to solving these problems lies in the transformation and development of China's national economy. Therefore, if we want the proper development of society, we must first lay down all the conditions for developing the national economy. At the same time, we should not adopt the principles of capitalism, but take the state's operation as the center of the economy, creating the requirements of the economy on the one hand, and restricting private capital development and gradually moving towards a society of common production on the other hand. This is the trend of China's economy today. In this transformation of the national economy, the masses should naturally be given the opportunity to participate in production management to accelerate the improvement of the masses' lives. Guaranteeing all survival rights and raising the level of general culture are the contents of building a national economy. Only then can we talk about the people's livelihood today, otherwise, everything is empty talk.

(4) Education Issue: Education is a right that everyone should enjoy. Therefore, it is not enough to only receive general education and compulsory education to be equal. Higher education is also something that everyone should enjoy. However, in a commodity production society, apart from a few people who can receive higher education, most people can only sigh at the top universities. Even compulsory education may not be affordable for ordinary people. The children of ordinary people reach the age of education, but they cannot go to school because they do not have the leisure to study. They need to earn some money to supplement their family's livelihood. Therefore, equal educational opportunities seem to be just empty words. If we want equal education, we must first eliminate the obstacles that prevent equal education.

(5) Women's Issue: The women's issue is not a special issue. The liberation of Chinese women and the liberation of the entire nation cannot be separated. However, in China, there is an extra layer of traditional feudal constraints. Generally speaking, women's status in society is different from men's. Therefore, we should specifically protect the status of women in the Constitution.

The above are just a few main issues. Because the editor drafted the manuscript hastily and the space is limited, there are bound to be omissions. Fortunately, the purpose of this article is to contribute a little guidance for readers' research. The real research still needs to be done by the readers themselves and cannot be satisfied with the shallow description in this article.

Spring and Autumn

Records of Lingering Imperial Fragrance 209

— Written for this publication by Princess Der Ling

Preface

Princess Der Ling once wrote the book "Two Years in the Forbidden City", which has long been popular. Later, while she was in the United States, she heard that publications were circulating, but because she was separated by the ocean, she had not had the opportunity to see them, which was her greatest regret. Last year, I saw her new book "Imperial Incense" and read it through. It is no less than an unofficial history of Empress Dowager Cixi. Being a blood-related sister separated from her by thousands of miles, I cannot help but feel a sense of the division of our family. Judging from her structure and style, Rong Ling can only look up to her, like Ziyou and Zixia, I dare not utter a word of praise. However, some of the events listed in the book are described in such flowery language, like mirages, making them intangible. As my conscience dictates, I will try to verify them. For example, regarding the section on Empress Dowager Cixi and Ronglu, after checking the records, Empress Dowager Cixi entered the palace at the age of sixteen. At that time, Ronglu was serving outside and was still a child. They had never met face-to-face, so where did the love come from? In the tenth year of the Republic, General Joffre of France came to China. Rong Ling was among those who prepared for the reception. The float he rode in Tianjin was the one mentioned in the book. In fact, after the float was made, Empress Dowager Cixi never had the opportunity to ride in it. As for the palace shoemaker and other matters, they are even more fictitious. After checking, the Empress's shoes were always made by the wives of the princes and nobles. Recalling the Xuantong era, my sister and I entered and exited the palace and served the Empress for the longest time. However, my sister left the palace before the Empress passed away, and Rong Ling left the palace after the Empress passed away. The difference between them was three or four years. As for the minute details of the forbidden city, Rong Ling seems to know them more accurately. Therefore, I will not hesitate to provide a clear testimony to help my sister collect the relics of the previous dynasty. If this book is novel and exciting, it can be read as a novel for leisure and entertainment. But if it is regarded as a record of events, then it is half a mirage, empty and untrue, and it inevitably hurts loyalty and honesty. Remembering Mr. Cai Yuanpei's "A Dream of Red Mansions" research, which details the story of Dong Xiaowan, his moral character and writings are admirable. Moreover, Rong Ling cannot help but speak out for my beloved sister. I offer my sincerity. Let De Sister be the judge of my guilt.

Furthermore, Rong Ling is currently compiling a book in English about the events of the late Ming Dynasty and has no free time. After I finish my work, I will carefully verify each item in English to let European and American readers understand the truth of this book. Because Mr. Qin is translating and publishing it, I will briefly mention a few points as a token of responsibility.

"Qingming" 210

— Huo Xueming

The season when parasol trees are in bloom, peach blossoms are in full bloom, and rapeseed flowers are brilliantly yellow; when swallows fly back and forth in the tender breeze of willows – these are the characteristics of "Qingming."

In our villages, during this period, every family invites relatives for a big feast at home. Even poor families will borrow money to hold one. Because farmers, merchants, and artisans are busy all year round and rarely have the chance to meet each other, this opportunity allows them to "narrate emotions in a secluded manner." Think about the many festivals passed down from ancestors; on a specific day, each family relies on superstitious customs to eat pastries, such as zongzi for the Dragon Boat Festival and cakes for the Double Ninth Festival. In fact, this is entirely because the wise people of that time felt sorry for the dull and frugal lives of farmers, merchants, and artisans; they came up with this method of adjustment. The meaning of Qingming is definitely not entirely about superstition. Secondly, Qingming is a festival when travelers yearn for their hometowns, and everyone thinks of their hometown, returning to visit the tombs of their ancestors. At the same time, they enjoy a day of reminiscing in the clan temple, with "young and old gathered together," discussing everything related to the clan. If they encounter complicated matters and do not have the money to seek legal remedies, they often rely on the collective opinion in the clan temple to determine right and wrong. Moreover, both parties cannot resist and will definitely not resist.

From this, we can experience that the intrinsic function of "Qingming" is twofold: first, it shows the people's initiative in uniting scattered emotions; second, it shows that the people can also handle their own disputes.

If someone can promote this kind of festival gathering, and encourage and expand it, I personally believe that the effectiveness of this organization is more powerful than wildly shouting slogans!

The Mentally Ill are True Heroes 211

— He Ru

The Eugenics Society raised the plan and question of eradicating epilepsy and madness. After expert research, it was felt that this kind of neurological disease makes a great contribution to human progress. An examination of the world's great achievers reveals that many suffer from mental illness. George Ives and Muhammad suffered from mental illness; Napoleon I, Alexander, and Saint Paul suffered severely from it. If there had been an Eugenics Society in ancient times that implemented its treatment procedures, I am afraid that most of the great heroes in history would have been lost, and the progress of society would be very different from what it is today. Currently, the German government castrates both men and women suffering from epilepsy, madness, and infectious diseases. The intention is solely for improving the breed. However, like Sima Qian writing the "Historical Records" and Wei Zhongxian comparing himself to Confucius, castration cannot resist the spread of erroneous ideas. Originally, a genius scholar, a creative master, must have the function of his nervous system to express his great fantasies. If the French Rousseau had not suffered from nerve degeneration, he would never have been able to produce the "Social Contract." If the German Marx had not suffered from extreme madness, he would never have been able to produce "Das Kapital." But all geniuses and great men have inextricably linked themselves with mental illness. In the theory of scientific improvement methods, it is to be regarded as the product of sin and the source of poison. But in the explanation of the principles of hereditary diseases, it is certain and unshakable, and has a very great effect. This is what I recognize as the mentally ill being true heroes. A unique and startling conclusion.

Everyone is Singing the Song of Military Reduction 212

Four Company Commanders in the Northeast 213

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twenty-Six

Generously Baring One's Heart, Forgetting the Family to Serve the Country

Sadly Facing the Jade Mirror, Lamenting My Waiting Man

The rain on the roof, pattered and hissed, making one feel the cold air invading the room, chilling from the legs straight to the waist. Not to mention how cold the air was, even the covered kerosene lamp on the table emitted a blue light, constantly sinking downwards. The wind in the sky, carrying raindrops, beat against the window lattices, especially where there were paper holes, through which the evening breeze drilled in, attacking the body, creating a feeling of desolation. After a while, the raindrops grew larger, pattering sporadically on the window, further causing one to feel endless sorrow. Thus, one propped one's head with one's hand, leaning against the table and sitting. The items on this long table were all gifts given when one got married, namely a pair of vases, a small clock, and a round mirror with a carved flower frame. The carved flower frames were all in the style of hollowed-out clouds, just like holding up a moon in the middle. One remembers that on the wedding night, two bright red candles were lit, shining brightly, reflecting the red light in the mirror, making one feel that the room was filled with joy. But now the joy has disappeared, leaving only the small kerosene lamp with its bean-sized flame, illuminating the room dimly. One remembers when Ziqiang was at home, one would sit and look in the mirror, one's face red and white, and Ziqiang would lean behind one's shoulder, looking into the mirror, laughing at one. But now, one is alone guarding this house, alone facing this mirror, and moreover, the mirror is dim and without light, and one cannot even see one's own reflection. If it were an ordinary family, at this time, the newly married couple would still be in their sweet period, but what about oneself? One is guarding an empty house. Because that night, one sighed deeply, and one's father-in-law heard it, causing him great worry, so he let oneself go to Beijing City. If one were to sigh again, adding to the father-in-law's worries, he would have to comfort me on behalf of his son. (351)

The Calendar Pages are Being Torn Off 214

— Rong Yu

When I get up every morning, without washing my face or rinsing my mouth, I mechanically glance at the calendar on the wall, and then quickly use two fingers to pinch it, and with a "tearing" sound, tear off yesterday's page. Perhaps this has become a habit of mine; every day when I get up, I must first tear off the calendar. I tear off one page after another, tearing away much time; tearing away several years; also tearing away the innocence of childhood; and also tearing away the lively youth; now it has been torn to the middle age with heavy forehead wrinkles. Keep tearing, tearing, tearing until the head is bald and the teeth are loose; the back is bent and hunched over; tear straight until "both hands are stretched out and both eyes are closed" and I can no longer tear. I think that tearing the calendar is a common thing, but it also contains the "process of life" and the "philosophy of life."

The calendar of the Republic of China, year 23. Tearing, tearing, three months have already been torn off, and there are still a thick nine months left, and I don't know how many patterns will be torn out. When I first had the knowledge to tear the calendar, I was still a loyal subject of the Great Qing Emperor, tearing, tearing, tearing away my thin braid; and tearing away the fate of Xuantong. After the establishment of the Republic, I tear the calendar every day, and every day there are new patterns to see, "North-South War," "Hongxian's Enthronement," "Zhang Xun's Restoration," and even the World War, all reflected with the pages of the calendar. The revolution was successful, and another anniversary was added to the calendar. However, the blows given by "September 18th" and "January 28th" also engraved the deepest and greatest painful marks on our calendar. Tearing, tearing, the years to come, the days of the future, one page after another are behind, I only hope that one page after another of the calendar will tear away our shame, tear away our trauma, and tear out a colorful picture of national prosperity and peace.

Miscellaneous Talk

Research on Inkstones (10) (5) 215

— Wuliao Ke

General Overview of Duan Inkstones

(5) The Value of Duan Inkstones: The above is a very brief overview of Duan inkstones, only discussing the points that those who study Duan inkstones must know. As for the former people's perspective on observing inkstones, and the basis for evaluating them, there are many differences, resulting in a lot of conflicting discussions, each holding their own opinion, forming a kind of faction, such as the dispute between new pits and old pits, the dispute between Zi stone and mountain stone; the dispute between valuing the ancient and valuing the modern; the dispute between valuing literature and valuing practicality; the dispute between the east cave and the west cave; the dispute between tenderness and firmness; the dispute between sound and silence; each has become a point of contention. Babbling and endless, how ridiculous this is! Although I am bored, I do not want to be verbose. However, there is still the question of the value of inkstones, and the high and low values are closely related to the purchasers of inkstones, so I will briefly say a few words.

The ancients described Duan inkstones as "worth a city" and "difficult to exchange for ten thousand gold," but only to describe their preciousness, not that they actually have such value. Su Yijian's "Inkstone Spectrum" says: "A naturally round and upright bluish-purple Zi stone from Duanxi, carved into an inkstone, can be worth a thousand gold," which seems more certain. However, this kind of Zi stone is ultimately difficult to obtain, and there is no certain value. Also, after checking Tao Fang's "Inkstone History," it says: "I have seen about five to seven hundred Duan inkstones in my life, and they are priceless above ten thousand," and Yunlin's "Stone Spectrum" says: "Pure Duan stones are also no more than ten thousand." It can be seen that the price of inkstones before the Qing Dynasty was not very high. Wu Shihua occasionally said the sentence: "Today's Laokeng Daxi Cave is ten times more valuable than Xiaoxi Cave Zhengdong stone, Xiaoxi Cave Zhengdong is ten times more valuable than Dongdong stone, and Kengziyan, Mazi Keng, and Chaotianyan decrease in order, but they are still several times higher than miscellaneous pits," (see Wu Lanxiu's "History of Duanxi Inkstones") and the Japanese have taken this seriously and calculated it. He said:

According to Wu's words, if the words "several times" are set as five times, for example, if an inkstone produced from a miscellaneous pit is worth one yuan, the one produced from Chaotianyan is worth five yuan, the one produced from Mazi Keng is worth six yuan, the one produced from Kengziyan is worth seven yuan, and the Dongdong is about twice as high as Kengziyan, so it is worth fourteen yuan. Xiaoxi Cave Zhengdong is calculated at ten times, then it is one hundred and forty yuan. If Daxi Cave is calculated at ten times more, it would be one thousand four hundred yuan. The famous materials of the true Daxi Cave are indeed very precious, and there is no need to say more about the Xiayan of the Song Dynasty. (See Ko Kaga's "Inkstone Talk")

Such a calculation shows that in the minds of the Japanese, the value of Duan inkstones is very high, and there are many Japanese inkstone enthusiasts. According to his boastful tone, "Many of the famous Chinese inkstones are now collected by Japanese inkstone lovers. The inkstone lovers in Tokyo have more insight than those in Kyoto and Osaka, and are richer in collecting famous inkstones. As for calligraphers and painters, for practical use, they feel that Duan inkstones are a hundred times better than Japanese inkstones, so they do not hesitate to raise huge sums of money to acquire them." The price of Chinese inkstones has been raised so high, which cannot be counted as the effort of the Japanese.

The general overview of Duan inkstones is finished, and below I will talk about She inkstones.

Another Unfortunate Incident in the Football World; Eastern China vs. Western Concession Ends with No Result 221

Both Sides Act Out of Bounds; Referee Misjudges Offside

Referee Leaves the Field Because Players Do Not Accept Punishment

Yesterday, in the Western Concession's Western Union Football League's Group A match at the China Baseball Field, an unfortunate incident occurred. The first half passed peacefully, but in the second half, after playing for fifteen minutes, Lu Zhongen took four steps while holding the ball. The referee blew the whistle and awarded a free kick. Chen Hongguang of Eastern China seemed to have a disrespectful attitude towards the referee. The referee expelled him from the field (because Chen had previously received a warning). Eastern China asked the referee to announce the reason, but the referee did not say why and resolutely left the field. The game ended with no result. Subsequently, there was a refund craze.

Acting Out of Bounds

The main cause of the turmoil was due to the excessive behavior of both sides. Referee Sinclair, the center forward of the Western Concession team, is also a newly appointed referee. The penalties imposed in the first half were considered appropriate, but in the second half, he became more and more strict, but the two offsides he judged against Eastern China were a bit off, causing dissatisfaction from Eastern China and the audience. At the same time, the actions of both sides became more and more blatant, and the grievances deepened. Fallas of the Western Concession and Chen Hongguang of Eastern China were each warned once, and the degree of out-of-bounds kicking was the same for both sides.

Each Scores a Draw 222

In the first half, things were initially peaceful, and the game was very exciting. Later, suspicions gradually arose, and everyone had the intention of harming each other. Fortunately, the referee's strict penalties were able to end things peacefully. The Western Concession scored the first goal, which Fallas scored from 30 yards out. The ball landed and rolled quickly, and Lu Zhongen missed and let it in. But after the kickoff, Eastern China went straight to the yellow dragon, and Jia Youliang's header was kicked into his own goal by Fallas. Eastern China then made the result 1-1.

Each Receives a Warning 223

Starting in the second half, the referee's inspection became stricter, but the rude behavior of both sides became more blatant. The referee judged Wan Xianghua's two offsides, (it seemed that Li Rongan and Wan also had one or two in the first half) which seemed to be a misjudgment, causing dissatisfaction from Eastern China and disturbances from the audience. Fallas and Chen Hongguang were both warned for misconduct, and the atmosphere in the stadium deteriorated.

Disobeying the Referee 224

Unexpectedly, after fifteen minutes, Lu Zhongen took four steps while holding the ball. The referee imposed a free kick as required, at a location five or six yards to the right corner of the goal. However, Chen Hongguang seemed to have a disrespectful expression towards the referee. The referee expelled him from the field. Lu Zhongen and Feng, the linesman of Eastern China, questioned the reason, but the referee did not answer and left the field abruptly. The game was abandoned halfway. How this matter will end depends on the solution of the Western Union Association.

Refund Craze 225

The audience was in an uproar, but everyone stood still and did not leave, because they did not know the whole story. After waiting for a long time and the game did not continue, they asked for refunds one after another. The French police originally dispatched dozens of detectives and police officers to the scene, and seeing the situation, they dispatched a large number of police officers to maintain order. The head of the Western detectives and the chief patrolman of the police station personally led them to the scene. The Sports Federation hurriedly handled the refund procedures. It was estimated that only more than 200 tickets for the one-yuan seat were sold, but more than 600 tickets were refunded. More than 2,000 tickets for the four-corner seat were refunded, reaching more than 3,000 tickets. It can be said to be an unexpected disaster.

Chinese Basketball Court Completely Destroyed by Fire 238

Fire broke out at approximately 11 PM last night; cause unknown.

The French Concession Fire Brigade responded to the scene to extinguish the fire.

The Chinese Basketball Court on Rue Father Lebbe in the French Concession, part of the Shanghai National Amateur Athletic Federation's sports grounds, was the largest indoor basketball court in Shanghai. The internal stands could accommodate 1,500 to 2,000 spectators. Unfortunately, at around 11 PM last night, it was suddenly visited by the Fire God and completely destroyed. The entire French Concession Fire Brigade was dispatched and did its utmost to extinguish the fire, but because the entire structure was made of wood, the flames were extraordinary, leaving only an empty shell. After three quarters of an hour, the fire gradually weakened.

Speculations on the Cause of the Fire 239

Yesterday at 6 PM, the Shanghai basketball team, preparing to participate in the national preliminary round for the Far Eastern Games, practiced at the court. Afterwards, a foreign basketball team practiced. It was discovered that the fire started in the restroom next to the bathing room. The surroundings of the room were filled with bamboo scraps, wood shavings, reed mats, and other flammable materials. The cause of the fire is generally believed to be that basketball players carelessly discarded cigarette butts while using the restroom, which ignited the fire.

Zhang Huiqing Awakened in Shock from a Dream 240

Zhang Huiqing, an employee of the Amateur Athletic Federation, lived with his family of seven inside the basketball court. Servants Wan Zhao and Fulin also lived there. Fulin was still in the writing room, while the rest were fast asleep and completely unaware of the fire. Fortunately, a gentleman from Yuzhen Lane across the street saw the fire in the building and immediately knocked on the door to wake Zhang and the others, allowing them to escape. However, their belongings could not be retrieved.

A Brief History of the Basketball Court’s Construction 241

The basketball court was built as far back as ten years ago, managed by a Westerner named Gray. Since the Amateur Athletic Federation took over in 1925, it has been repeatedly repaired and the stands expanded, making it the only great indoor basketball court in Shanghai today. Men's and women's basketball competitions are held every year. The national basketball selection for this year's Far Eastern Games was also scheduled to be held at the court. Unexpectedly, it was completely destroyed by fire last night. The location for the selection of the Chinese basketball team will have to be arranged elsewhere.

Local News

Shanghai Branch of the China Cultural Construction Association Established Yesterday 247

More Than 300 Members of Groups and Individuals Attended

Charter Passed and Directors and Councilors Elected

The Shanghai Branch of the China Cultural Construction Association held its inaugural meeting at the Huzhou Society on Guizhou Road at 2 PM yesterday. Details are as follows:

Attending Members: Attendees included Wu Xingya, representative of the Municipal Government; Tao Baichuan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters; Pan Gonglu, representative of the General Association; members Wu Kaixian, Zhang Shiyong, Li Zhaozhong, Huang Zhaoxiong, Wang Yunwu, Ma Chonggan, Lin Zhongke, Pei Fuheng, Fan Zhongyun, Zhang Zhuping, Meng Shouchun, Chen Jicheng, Lu Shibai, Jiang Jianbai, Wang Xinming, Xu Ze , Tang Zeng, Xu Xingchu, Xu Zejun, Wang Longzhang, Han Juemin, Liang Shaowen, He Xiya, Xu Zhuodai, Zhang Yiping, Shao Zuiweng, Chen Dongbai, Zhu Ying , Liu Xiuru, Ding Mocun, Chen Jinmin, Wu Zhiqian, Chen Bai, and group members including the Opera Discussion Society, Municipal Education Association, Greater Education Federation, Chinese Education Federation, University Federation, Modern Thought Society, Southwest Review Society, Micro-speech Weekly Society, Lion's Roar Literary Society, Literary Spring and Autumn Society, Foreign Affairs Society, and Courage Society, totaling more than 300 people.

Chairman’s Report: The presidium consisted of Zhang Shiyong, Zhang Zhuping, Fan Zhongyun, Ding Mocun, Wang Xinming, Lin Zhongke, Jiang Jianbai, Chen Jicheng, and Pei Fuheng, totaling nine people. Tang Zeng served as recorder, and Shen Zurui as master of ceremonies. After completing the ceremonial formalities, Chairman Jiang Jianbai gave a report, stating that the association was established in accordance with the charter of the General Association and based on the Three Principles of the People to build a new Chinese culture. The colleagues felt that the environment in Shanghai was complex and cultural construction was needed, making it more important than any other place. China's current culture has not been organized for its inherent aspects, nor has it applied what is needed from foreign sources. Therefore, the culture that China needs still lacks solid construction, and the survival of the nation depends entirely on culture, highlighting the importance of the cultural mission, especially in Shanghai, where trends are disseminated. Therefore, this association was established today in accordance with the charter of the General Association and will follow the guidance of the General Association and the instructions of party and government agencies to work for the revitalization of Chinese culture.

Address by the Party Headquarters: Tao Baichuan, representative of the Municipal Party Headquarters, delivered an address, stating that there are two important points to building a Chinese culture that is suitable for the times, which he would like to offer to everyone. The first point is not to forget the spirit of the nation, and the second point is not to forget the spirit of the times. A culture that can be built to simultaneously include the national spirit and the spirit of the times is the culture that China needs. Looking back at China’s past thousands of years, there has been a very glorious culture. However, because the ancients did not organize it, later scholars have largely neglected China’s inherent culture, believing that foreign culture is superior to China. Currently, the political science, economics, sociology, and education studied in general schools all introduce Western ideas, while China’s inherent ideas cannot be known for their strengths due to the poor organization work. Students do not look for cultural ideas in ancient Chinese books. Therefore, besides the ideas created by foreigners, they do not know that China has had many excellent cultures in the past that also meet the needs of the times. If we do not do this promotional work, it will definitely decline in the future. Therefore, it is hoped that in one or two years, due to the establishment of the China Cultural Construction Association, the first step will be the publication of books on various political, economic, social, and educational subjects that integrate Chinese and Western knowledge, so that future generations will know the greatness of China's institutions and that China also has things worth studying. Therefore, it is hoped that the Cultural Construction Association will organize China's past history, not forget the spirit of the nation and the spirit of the times. As for Western culture, such as social organizational power, material civilization, and scientific spirit, which are lacking in our country, we should catch up with the spirit of catching up and absorb them as much as possible. We should use scientific methods as the principle of building culture, so that the nation and the times are combined to produce a new culture. Therefore, the organization of the association must be to work together to formulate cultural plans and cultural work.

Address by the General Association: Pan Gongzhan, representative of the General Association, delivered an address, stating that the General Association of the China Cultural Construction Association was established not long ago, and seeing the establishment of the branch today has greatly increased the courage of the comrades of the General Association to engage in culture. The center of gravity of the China Cultural Construction Association is entirely in Shanghai, so the headquarters of the General Association is also located in Shanghai. However, the work of the General Association must also take into account other provinces and cities, so the Shanghai branch is expected to shoulder the burden of the Shanghai side. How the General Association's achievements will be demonstrated in the future depends on how the Shanghai branch performs. The undertakings that the association should handle are stated in the charter, such as publication, news, education, film, opera, fine arts, music, and other matters related to the nation are included. It is hoped that the groups or individuals who join the association will all make efforts in their original research undertakings in accordance with the purpose of building a new Chinese culture based on the Three Principles of the People. However, all previous individuals or groups doing cultural work lacked a center. After the establishment of this association, it is hoped that the previous disorganized, unregulated, and independent cultural work will be changed into planned cooperation, and that the Shanghai cultural community will plan a unified solution.

List of Staff: Following the passage of the charter, directors and councilors were discussed. Those elected were: Tao Baichuan as Director-General, Jiang Jianbai and Wang Xinming as Deputy Directors-General, and Zhang Jixin, Chen Baohua, Jian Wanqiu, Shen Zurui, Du Gang, Huang Jingzhai, Xue Guangqian, Gu Jiwu, Yi Lirong, Yao Sufeng, Zhang Renruo, Lin Meiyan, Xu Suling, Huang Hao, Tang Zhengyang, Liu Xiuru, Xu Zexiang, Xu Shifu, and Yuan Xueyi as Directors. The elected councilors were Xiao Youmei, Wang Jiyuan, Lu Bin, Shen Junsheng, Zhou Xianwen, Zhu Zhangbao, Fan Zhongyun, Qiu Hanping, Chen Jinmin, Lu Yinquan, Li En , Chen Zehua, Chen Gaorong, Zhang Shilu, Shao Zuiweng, Yang Minshi, Huang Zhaoxiong, Leng Xueqiao, Kang Xuanyi, Chen Jicheng, Yuan Yeyu, Gu Zhongyi, Wang Zhongxian, Chen Jilie, Shen Songquan, Dai Pengtian, Xu Xingchu, Chen Kecheng, He Xiya, Wang Hanzhang, Zhang Yiping, Tang Jinbai, Zhou Leshan, Huang Xianggu, Bu Wancang, Zhao Shusheng, and Zhu Xuefan, totaling 37 people.

Various Cultural Organizations Hosted a Banquet for Albert Thomas Last Night 251

More than 100 people including Li Shizeng and Wu Tiecheng attended

Thomas gave a speech on the mission of intellectual laborers

Twelve organizations, including the World Cultural Cooperation China Association, the National Central Research Institute, the National Peiping Research Institute, the National Jinan University, the World Electrical Engineering Society, the China International Library, the Sino-French University, the Sino-French Industrial School, the World Academy, the Library Publishing School, the World Society, and the Shanghai Municipal Government, hosted a banquet for Albert Thomas, Director of the International Labour Office, at the World Society on Ferguson Road last night at 7:00 p.m. During the banquet, Li Shizeng introduced Thomas's speech, entitled "The Mission of Intellectual Laborers in Modern Life," and the Datong Orchestra performed national music. Details are as follows:

Attendees: A total of more than 100 people attended, including Li Shizeng, Cai Yuanpei, Wu Tiecheng, Liu Zhanen, Li Shuhua, Chu Minyi, Ding Xielin, Wang Xiaolai, Li Denghui, Shi Liangcai, Zhang Junqi, Hua Lin, Yang Yunzhong, Lin Yutang, Shen Pengfei, Zhuang Wenya, Yang Guangzhe, Du Chongda, Chen Hexian, Hu Tianshi, Cui Lian, Yu Hongjun, Li Dachao, Chen Guangfu, Ye Yuhu, Weng Zhilong, Wang Yunwu, Wu Yunshu, Zhang Zhuping, Wang Boqi, Liu Hongsheng, and foreign guests such as the French Minister and the Dutch Minister.

Chairman's Speech: First, Chairman Li Shizeng gave an introductory speech, saying that today they were welcoming Mr. Albert Thomas and, at the same time, saying farewell to Mr. Thomas because Mr. Thomas would be leaving China in the shortest possible time. Mr. Thomas is a famous educator and also the Director of the International Labour Office. It is a rare opportunity to have Mr. Thomas come to the meeting to give a speech today.

Thomas's Speech: Next, Albert Thomas gave a speech, translated by Zhang Junqi, entitled "The Mission of Intellectual Laborers in Modern Life." He briefly stated that the question of the mission of intellectual laborers is very serious and is related to the maintenance of civilization and the maintenance of life. However, the general public has two attitudes towards this question: (1) to despise intellectual laborers, and (2) to value intellectual laborers. Leaving aside the latter, the reason for the former's contempt for intellectual labor is that modern people, due to material civilization, do not have much time for intellectual life, and in the current environment, it is not suitable for the life of intellectuals. In fact, this view is completely wrong. All material inventions are full of wisdom and full of brainpower. For example, the invention of machines is by no means a mere fantasy; it must come from wisdom. Modern life has two foundations: (1) hygiene, and (2) education. Hygiene and education are nothing but intellectual work. France divides mankind into three classes: (1) capitalists, (2) laborers, and (3) intellectuals. This classification is also incorrect because there are many intellectuals among laborers, so labor and wisdom cannot be separated. As for the mission of intellectual laborers, in addition to applying it to practical problems, it must also be extended to society, the country, and the international community. There are many international disputes in modern times, and the reason is that the wisdoms are different and cannot be understood. In the future, only the intellectual circles can unite, exchange opinions, and study problems together so that there is no barrier between countries. The League of Nations has established an International Cultural Cooperation Association to undertake this work. The Chinese side has also established the China Association, which has a great deal of strength. At the same time, the treatment and status of intellectuals should be improved. Therefore, the International Labour Office has organized an Intellectuals Committee, whose work is to improve the lives and status of intellectuals.

Musical Performance: After Thomas's speech, the Datong Orchestra, led by ancient music expert Zheng Qinwen, performed national music. The program was as follows: (1) Ensemble performance of Oriental Great Music; (2) Jin Zuli's pipa solo, entitled "Frontier Tune"; (3) Wei Zhongle's guqin solo, entitled "Drunk Fisherman's Evening Song," which was extremely subtle and exquisite. The event did not end until around 9:00 p.m.

Special Feature

Three Opinions on the Contribution of National Education to the First Draft of the Constitution (Middle) Xie Engao 253

2. Compulsory education and adult literacy education must be provided free of charge. Compulsory education has long been regarded as a national education policy in various countries. Since the rise of nationalism, this type of education has been included in the powers of the state. Therefore, although there are many meanings of compulsory education, the most important is the meaning that "the state has the obligation to provide the necessary resources and facilities for the minimum national education and to use legal force to compel all school-age children in the country to receive training." Since the state has the responsibility and obligation to provide this type of education, it should not collect any fees. The reason is very clear; otherwise, not only will the national education policy not be implemented and the original intention of compulsory education will be lost, but also the promotion of compulsory education will be hindered, and the goal of universalization will be difficult to achieve. After the implementation of the New Economic Policy in Soviet Russia, tuition fees were once collected, but they were soon abolished. Other countries in the world, except for the Netherlands, almost all provide compulsory education free of charge. Those that state this in their constitutions, such as Spain, stipulate that primary education is free of charge; Portugal stipulates that compulsory primary education is implemented and no tuition fees are charged; Turkey stipulates that the provision of primary education is generally not remunerated; Lithuania stipulates that primary education is free of charge in schools established by the state or autonomous bodies; Greece stipulates that primary education is compulsory and should be paid for by the state; Finland stipulates that education in primary schools is free for everyone; Poland stipulates that national and local public schools are exempt from tuition fees; Estonia stipulates that primary schools are free, etc., all of which can be verified. Compulsory education and primary schools in China have always been one. Although Article 16 of the Primary School Law promulgated by the National Government clearly stipulates that "primary schools do not charge tuition fees," it is followed by the phrase "but may charge fees as appropriate depending on local conditions." Thus, the principle established is tantamount to a fundamental overthrow, so that most primary schools today still collect fees arbitrarily and even have something to rely on. In Nanjing and Shanghai, one is the capital and the other is a commercial metropolis. Educational funds should be easier to raise than in the interior. However, primary school tuition fees have not only not been waived, but the amount collected often exceeds the fixed amount by several times, which is tantamount to imposing additional taxes on those who fulfill their obligations, which is very regrettable. Article 35 of the chapter on education in this draft constitution stipulates that "the people of the Republic of China have equal opportunities to receive education," which seems to have taken into account the current trend of equal educational opportunities. However, China's social and economic decline has reached an extreme, and most people are unable to provide adequate food and clothing, making it difficult to force them to bear their children's tuition fees in reality. If schools are still allowed to charge fees freely, although opportunities are equal, those who actually enjoy them may never have the hope of equality. Judging from the current state of the country, it would be unrealistic to make all levels of schools free of charge. However, compulsory education is the foundation of national education. In order to realize the national education policy and facilitate its implementation, it must be absolutely stipulated that no fees of any kind should be charged, so as to prevent the habit of charging fees as a principle and free of charge as an exception from occurring in various places in the future. As for adult literacy education, it is a remedial measure for the military and the illiterate. The objects of this type of education are all people who were born poor and lost the opportunity to enjoy compulsory education in their youth. The state should also stipulate that it should be provided free of charge, so as to eliminate illiteracy throughout the country as soon as possible.

The Quantity of Yarn Purchased by Yunnan and Guangdong Gangs is Still Good 255

丨丨Due to Competitive Sales, Selling Prices are Instead Cheaper丨丨

The yarn market rose in the morning and fell in the afternoon, and the situation was extremely decadent. Due to the deterioration of the surrounding environment, all kinds of prices are trending down. As a result, the sales of cotton yarn are declining, and all parties lack purchasing power, which has led to a gradual increase in the manufacturer's inventory. However, the Yunnan gang is still healthy in its appetite, but the selling prices are 2.5 to 5 jiao cheaper due to the competitive sales of various factories.

Marker Yarn is Slack 256

The market of marker yarn opened in the morning, and the popularity was slightly boosted due to the rise in US cotton. Each month rose by three or seven jiao. In the afternoon, there was a lack of sellers in the market, and the spot yarn market price was soft again, and the selling wind rose again. Each month rose by five, seven, eight, and nine jiao to one yuan. The total transaction volume for the day was 21,800 bales. Dafeng bought 1,000 bales, Gengfeng 650 bales, Chunj 550 bales, Suilong 550 bales, Changfeng 2,500 bales, and Yuantai 500 bales. Pessimistic Northeast Cotton Yarn and Cloth Market 262

According to Mr. Okuri of the Dalian branch of a certain Japanese trading company, the trend of the cotton yarn industry in Northeast China depends entirely on how the sales of agricultural products are. The prices of agricultural products have plummeted this year, and farmers are extremely impoverished. The purchasing power of cotton yarn and cloth has naturally declined. According to the current situation, it is difficult to be optimistic. General consumers only purchase necessary items. This is not only the case for cotton cloth, but also for Indian cotton yarn, which has little buying interest. Originally, when market prices fell, futures trading completely disappeared. The so-called inability to generate false demand can only supply a small amount of actual demand. The current sluggishness of cotton yarn and cloth is due to the fundamental reason that the countryside is declining, and the erosion of rayon is also one of the reasons. Recently, the demand for rayon has gradually increased.

Bombay Cotton Industry Weekly Report 263

The market was calm during the week. Brokers closed out long positions, inquiries about exports were disappointing, and exporters bought very little. However, Bai Luoxi cotton futures trading was quite active. The tax rate from the countryside to the city will be abolished on April 1. Therefore, the cumulative number of receipts announced between the 23rd and 26th of this month was 45,691 bales less than the same period last year. At the same time, the arrival of Bai Luoxi and Aomura was also less than last year. However, Kangtai and Xi Kangbudi and other flowers have begun to emerge.

Financial and Foreign Banks Closed, and the Chinese Financial Industry Market Was Depressed 264

Yesterday, the foreign exchange continued to trend downstream. Both the morning and afternoon markets opened at four points. Transfers plus water were not opened and done. It was all white transfers. The market atmosphere was loose and outrageous. The market for interbank lending was also relatively quiet. Interbank lending turnover was over 4.3 million in the morning market, new transactions were over 400,000, and turnover was over 200,000 in the afternoon market. Transactions in the small general assembly were over 300,000, transactions in foreign collateral were over 500,000, banknotes were recovered over 300,000, and the amount issued was over 700,000. The source of customer funds was only 150,000. Bank collections were rare because foreign merchants were still in the closed season and completely shut down. Only Chinese banks were conducting transactions as usual, and collections were also sparse. It is estimated that ticket collection was over 1.6 million, and various freight, exchange, tax collateral, and miscellaneous collections were less than 2 million. Warehouse withdrawals were 200,000, money shop foreign public single collections were over 35 million, various remittance funds were over 400,000, foreign transfer collections were over 2.1 million, and cash collections were over 100,000. In addition, the total number of exchanges at the Shanghai Clearing House on the 31st was 11,098,078.28 yuan in silver dollars, including 4,556,139.21 yuan in silver dollars and 6,541,939.07 yuan in exchange transfers.

Weak Fluctuation of Subsidiary Currency 265

Yesterday, the early market price for Jiangnan small silver coins was 833.5 yuan, an increase of 0.5 yuan compared to the previous day. The afternoon market price remained the same. The trading volume in the early market was 5,000 jiao, and in the afternoon market, it was 2,000 jiao. The price of copper coins increased by 500 wen, reaching 322,000 wen. The trading volume was 32,200 strings, equivalent to 10,000 yuan in silver.

Minimal Interest Rate Bottom Line 266

During the entire month of March, the call loan market for silver dollars was entirely "white lending" (lending without interest) for the first half of the month, with no market price at all. It was only from the 16th that a market price of 2 fen appeared. Therefore, the entire month only had half a month's worth of value, totaling no more than 5.4 jiao, with each day only amounting to slightly over 1.8 li. It is anticipated that the upcoming general meeting will propose interest rates, but the rate will likely remain fixed at 2.95 yuan after deductions. The sluggishness of silver funds can be seen from this.

Stable Situation of Rice in the River Downstream Grain Market 267

(Shanghai South) More than 40 sources of various merchant guilds (over 6,000 shi), with thick and thin japonica rice each accounting for half. In terms of sales destinations, late-season rice is more popular, although merchant guilds from other provinces have stopped buying, while those from Tianjin, Weihaiwei, and Yantai in northern China continue to show interest in purchasing. However, the situation is not as strong as it was a few days ago, likely because of initial rumors about a customs closure around the Gregorian calendar Qingming Festival, leading to some hesitation. Later, it was confirmed that customs would not be closed and would continue normal operations, so everyone started to be more proactive. As a result, the overall situation was slightly affected. In total, more than 2,000 packages of Qingjiao, Songsi, and Xilian rice were purchased. As for the issue of consumption, sellers took advantage of opportunities to drive up prices, so even though merchants still wanted to be demanding, they could not. The market situation is stable, with no significant price fluctuations. The stock of each merchant guild’s thick japonica rice has slightly improved, and the market situation seems to be tightening, but prices have not yet shown any significant changes. The goods from Changbang and Nangang are settled, while those from Sutongbang have seen a slight increase of 0.02 to 0.03 yuan due to the scarcity of goods. Du Yangjian and Yinbianyuan rice have not shown any significant fluctuations.

(Shanghai North) Yesterday, 42 or 43 boats arrived from various routes downstream of the river. Sales of various types of rice in the market remain lackluster. Prices for various types of rice, including white japonica, various grades of pointed rice, early thin rice, and Yinbianyuan rice, are fixed. White Yuan increased by 0.03 to 0.05 yuan.

Medium-Grain Rice from Other Provinces Continues to Rise by 0.05 Yuan 268

Yesterday, the market situation for medium-grain rice from other provinces continued to be strong, as Fujian merchants were actively buying. There was continued interest from the main street and Wenzhou. Although the purchases from Wenzhou were not as high as those from Fujian, they were consistent daily, which helped to stimulate the market. Yesterday, the entire city sold 6,310 packages of various types of rice. The main street purchased 200 packages, and Wenzhou purchased over 1,000 packages. The rest was all purchased by merchants from Fujian province. The main destination in Fujian was Fuzhou, with Xiamen only purchasing 220 packages. There was still a shortage of rice from Hunan and Jiangxi. Arrivals continued from Wuxi, Nanjing, Jiangbei, and Shashi, so the market could not rise significantly. Except for medium-grain rice from other provinces, which rose by 0.05 yuan due to active purchases from Fujian merchants, other types of rice remained stable.

Soybeans Rise by 0.03 to 0.04 Yuan 269

Yesterday, the soybean market saw a slight increase of 0.03 to 0.04 yuan due to limited new supplies and consistent sales from factories, with continued purchases from other merchants. However, future price fluctuations still depend on factory demand. Yesterday, factories purchased four truckloads of Yingzhou soybeans, Fujian merchants purchased one truckload of Zhushan soybeans, and the main street purchased 300 packages of Quanhe fertilizer soybeans and 200 packages of Quanhe soybeans, as well as two truckloads of Zhushan soybeans. Green soybeans are more stable than yellow soybeans and are considered specialty goods. Because supply and demand are evenly matched, the market price is quite firm. Yesterday, Ningbo merchants purchased 20 packages of Niuzhuang green soybeans and 200 packages of Guide green soybeans.

Silk and Tea: New York Silk Prices Fall Endlessly 270

(Record Low Discovered) New York in the United States has many silk weaving factories, making it the largest port for silk consumption in the world. Recently, due to sluggish sales of silk products, silk weaving factories have reduced production, cut working hours, and shut down machines, leading to a sharp decline in silk consumption. Furthermore, aggressive dumping of Japanese silk has caused silk prices to plummet endlessly. The standard raw silk (i.e., Japanese silk) has broken through the $1.30 USD per pound mark, equivalent to approximately 420 yuan per package (100 catties) in Chinese currency, reaching a new record low. Chinese silk, Shanghai white factory grade B, 80 points, 20-22 denier, is offered at 450-460 yuan (in Chinese currency), but there are no buyers. Qili dried spun silk has prices but no market. Since the beginning of spring, there have been no new transactions, and sales of Chinese silk to the United States have reached a dead end.

(Reverse Spun Silk Becomes Increasingly Scarce) Reverse spun silk produced in Mutown and Qingyang in Anhui Province is running out of stock at the production site, and sources are becoming increasingly scarce. Yesterday, only 26 pieces arrived from Datong and were awaiting sale on the pier.

(No Market for Foreign Silk on Christmas) Yesterday was Christmas Day (commonly referred to as Foreign Qingming). Foreign merchants and banks were closed, and there was no exchange market. Foreign firms are taking a four-day holiday as usual, and the foreign silk market is closed. Domestic silk factories are reluctant to purchase yellow and white spun silk from Jiangsu and Zhejiang due to high prices and are taking a wait-and-see approach. There is little news from the silk market.
